The game starts with highest double and then subsequent rounds start with next lower double.\r\n\r\nEach player has a private train where he/she can play a tile. There is one special train which can be played by any player. In each round a train must start with the rank of starting double of that round. In first turn players can play as many tiles as possible. From second turn onward players can only play one tile except when a double is played.
